- `github.com/sg-evals/client-go--v0.32.0` — use `repo:^github.com/sg-evals/client-go--v0.32.0$` filter

- `github.com/sg-evals/kubernetes--v1.32.0` — use `repo:^github.com/sg-evals/kubernetes--v1.32.0$` filter

Scope ALL keyword_search/nls_search queries to these repos.
Use the repo name as the `repo` parameter for read_file/go_to_definition/find_references.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# End-to-End: How Kubernetes Creates a Deployment

## Your Task

Explain how a Kubernetes client application creates a Deployment from start to finish. Trace through all three layers: 1. Client library — What type/function in `kubernetes-client-go` sends the HTTP request? 2. API server — What function in `kubernetes/kubernetes` receives and validates the create request? 3. Storage — What function in `etcd-io/etcd` persists the Deployment to the key-value store?

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the onboarding domain.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/etcd-io-etcd` (etcd-io/etcd)

## Summary

I've traced the complete flow through all three layers:

### **Layer 1: Client Library (client-go)**
- **File**: `kubernetes/typed/apps/v1/deployment.go`
- **Symbol**: `DeploymentInterface.Create()` and `rest.Post()`
- User calls `deploymentsClient.Create()` → Creates HTTP POST request via REST client

### **Layer 2: API Server (kubernetes)**
- **File**: `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/handlers/create.go`
- **Symbol**: `createHandler()` function (lines 53-237)
- Receives POST request, decodes the Deployment object, validates it, then delegates to storage layer via `REST.Create()`

### **Layer 3: Storage & etcd (etcd-io-etcd)**
- **File 1**: `server/etcdserver/api/v3rpc/key.go`
- **Symbol**: `kvServer.Put()` (lines 55-67)
- **File 2**: `server/etcdserver/v3_server.go`
- **Symbol**: `EtcdServer.Put()` (lines 139-146) and `RaftKV` interface
- Receives Put request, wraps it in RaftRequest, proposes to Raft consensus, applies to MVCC store, persists to bbolt backend

*EtcdServer) linearizableReadLoop() {\n815: \tfor {\n816: \t\trequestId := s.reqIDGen.Next()\n817: \t\tleaderChangedNotifier := s.LeaderChangedNotify()\n818: \t\tselect {\n819: \t\tcase {\n854: \t\t\tcase <-s.applyWait.Wait(confirmedIndex):\n855: \t\t\tcase <-s.stopping:\n856: \t\t\t\treturn\n857: \t\t\t}\n858: \t\t}\n859: \t\t// unblock all l-reads requested at indices before confirmedIndex\n860: \t\tnr.notify(nil)\n861: \t\ttrace.Step(\"applied index is now lower than readState.Index\")\n862: \n863: \t\ttrace.LogAllStepsIfLong(traceThreshold)\n864: \t}\n865: }\n866: \n867: func isStopped(err error) bool {\n868: \treturn err == raft.ErrStopped || err == ErrStopped\n869: }\n870: \n871: func (s *EtcdServer) requestCurrentIndex(leaderChangedNotifier <-chan struct{}, \n1019: func (s *EtcdServer) downgradeValidate(ctx context.Context, v string) (*pb.DowngradeResponse, error) {\n1020: \tresp := &pb.DowngradeResponse{}\n1021: \n1022: \ttargetVersion, err :=
